commit faef08cec3e11e1d2d0f0bd3ecf8d28771dc94ee
Author: Areeb Jamal <jamal.areeb@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Mar 25 04:06:32 2018 +0530

    fix: Remove loader based presenter injection (#834)
    
    Android guys, yet again changed the loader implementation,
    this time using LiveData and without telling anyone, introduced
    breaking changes. We were (wrongly) relying on `onStart` to
    get the presenter but in this update, the presenter started
    loading after `onStart` making the injected presenter null.
    
    - Remove loader based presenter injection
    - Presenters are created every time configuration is changed
    
    We will be moving towards ViewModel based implementation soon
